Section EsoIsEssentiallySurjective.
  Context {C₁ C₂ : bicat_of_univ_cats}
          {F : C₁ --> C₂}
          (HF : is_eso F).

  Let im : bicat_of_univ_cats := univalent_image F.
  Let fim : C₁ --> im := functor_full_img F.
  Let π : im --> C₂ := sub_precategory_inclusion _ _.

  
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
HF: is_eso F
im:= univalent_image F: bicat_of_univ_cats
fim:= functor_full_img F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, im ⟧
π:= sub_precategory_inclusion C₂
  (full_img_sub_precategory F): bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ im, C₂ ⟧
invertible_2cell (fim · π) (F · id₁ C₂)

invertible_2cell (fim · π) (F · id₁ C₂)

            π
            (fully_faithful_sub_precategory_inclusion _ _))
         fim
         (id₁ _)
         eso_is_essentially_surjective_inv2cell.

      exact (nat_z_iso_pointwise_z_iso

Section EssentiallySurjectiveIsEso.
  Context {C₁ C₂ : bicat_of_univ_cats}
          {F : C₁ --> C₂}
          (HF : essentially_surjective F).

  Section EssentiallySurjectiveEsoFull.
    Context {D₁ D₂ : bicat_of_univ_cats}
            {G : D₁ --> D₂}
            (HG : fully_faithful_1cell G)
            {H₁ H₂ : C₂ --> D₁}
            (n₁ : F · H₁ ==> F · H₂)
            (n₂ : H₁ · G ==> H₂ · G)
            (p : (n₁ ▹ G) • rassociator F H₂ G
                 =
                 rassociator F H₁ G • (F ◃ n₂)).

    Definition essentially_surjective_is_eso_lift_2_data
      : nat_trans_data (pr1 H₁) (pr1 H₂)
      := λ x, invmap
                (make_weq
                   _
                   (cat_fully_faithful_1cell_is_fully_faithful
                      _
                      HG
                      (pr1 H₁ x)
                      (pr1 H₂ x)))
                (pr1 n₂ x).

    
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
HF: essentially_surjective F
D₁, D₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
HG: fully_faithful_1cell G
H₁, H₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₂, D₁ ⟧
n₁: F · H₁ ==> F · H₂
n₂: H₁ · G ==> H₂ · G
p: (n₁ ▹ G) • rassociator F H₂ G =
rassociator F H₁ G • (F ◃ n₂)
is_nat_trans (pr1 H₁) (pr1 H₂)
  essentially_surjective_is_eso_lift_2_data

    
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
HF: essentially_surjective F
D₁, D₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
HG: fully_faithful_1cell G
H₁, H₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₂, D₁ ⟧
n₁: F · H₁ ==> F · H₂
n₂: H₁ · G ==> H₂ · G
p: (n₁ ▹ G) • rassociator F H₂ G =
rassociator F H₁ G • (F ◃ n₂)
is_nat_trans (pr1 H₁) (pr1 H₂)
  essentially_surjective_is_eso_lift_2_data

      
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
HF: essentially_surjective F
D₁, D₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
HG: fully_faithful_1cell G
H₁, H₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₂, D₁ ⟧
n₁: F · H₁ ==> F · H₂
n₂: H₁ · G ==> H₂ · G
p: (n₁ ▹ G) • rassociator F H₂ G =
rassociator F H₁ G • (F ◃ n₂)
x, y: C₂
f: C₂ ⟦ x, y ⟧
# (pr1 H₁) f
· essentially_surjective_is_eso_lift_2_data y =
essentially_surjective_is_eso_lift_2_data x
· # (pr1 H₂) f

      
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
HF: essentially_surjective F
D₁, D₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
HG: fully_faithful_1cell G

  Section EssentiallySurjectiveLift.
    Context {D₁ D₂ : bicat_of_univ_cats}
            {G : D₁ --> D₂}
            (HG : fully_faithful_1cell G)
            (H₁ : C₁ --> D₁)
            (H₂ : C₂ --> D₂)
            (α : invertible_2cell (H₁ · G) (F · H₂)).

    Let HG' : fully_faithful G
      := cat_fully_faithful_1cell_is_fully_faithful _ HG.
    Let α' : nat_z_iso (H₁ ∙ G) (F ∙ H₂)
      := invertible_2cell_to_nat_z_iso _ _ α.

    
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
HF: essentially_surjective F
D₁, D₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
HG: fully_faithful_1cell G
H₁: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, D₁ ⟧
H₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₂, D₂ ⟧
α: invertible_2cell (H₁ · G) (F · H₂)
HG':= cat_fully_faithful_1cell_is_fully_faithful G HG: fully_faithful G
α':= invertible_2cell_to_nat_z_iso (H₁ · G) (F · H₂) α: nat_z_iso (H₁ ∙ G) (F ∙ H₂)
y: pr1 C₂
isaprop (∑ x : pr1 D₁, z_iso (pr1 G x) (pr1 H₂ y))

    
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
HF: essentially_surjective F
D₁, D₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
HG: fully_faithful_1cell G
H₁: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, D₁ ⟧
H₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₂, D₂ ⟧
α: invertible_2cell (H₁ · G) (F · H₂)
HG':= cat_fully_faithful_1cell_is_fully_faithful G HG: fully_faithful G
α':= invertible_2cell_to_nat_z_iso (H₁ · G) (F · H₂) α: nat_z_iso (H₁ ∙ G) (F ∙ H₂)
y: pr1 C₂
isaprop (∑ x : pr1 D₁, z_iso (pr1 G x) (pr1 H₂ y))

      
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
HF: essentially_surjective F
D₁, D₂: bicat_of_univ_cats

(λ y : pr1 C₂, pr11 (iscontr_ob_fiber y)) y₂ ⟧

        exact (pr11 (iscontr_mor_fiber
                       g
                       (pr21 (iscontr_ob_fiber y₁))
                       (pr21 (iscontr_ob_fiber y₂)))).
    Defined.

α':= invertible_2cell_to_nat_z_iso (H₁ · G) (F · H₂) α: nat_z_iso (H₁ ∙ G) (F ∙ H₂)
y₁, y₂, y₃: pr1 C₂
g₁: pr1 C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
g₂: pr1 C₂ ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧
# (pr1 G)
  (pr11 (iscontr_mor_fiber g₁
           (pr21 (iscontr_ob_fiber y₁))
           (pr21 (iscontr_ob_fiber y₂))))
· (pr21 (iscontr_ob_fiber y₂) · # H₂ g₂) =
# G
  (pr11 (iscontr_mor_fiber g₁
           (pr21 (iscontr_ob_fiber y₁))
           (pr21 (iscontr_ob_fiber y₂))))
· (# G
     (pr11 (iscontr_mor_fiber g₂
              (pr21 (iscontr_ob_fiber y₂))
              (pr21 (iscontr_ob_fiber y₃))))
   · pr21 (iscontr_ob_fiber y₃))

        exact (pr21 (iscontr_mor_fiber

    Qed.

  (essentially_surjective_is_eso_lift HG H₁ H₂ α · G)
  H₂
 exact (essentially_surjective_is_eso_lift_right HG H₁ H₂ α).
    
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
HF: essentially_surjective F
D₁, D₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
HG: fully_faithful_1cell G
H₁: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, D₁ ⟧
H₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₂, D₂ ⟧
α: invertible_2cell (H₁ · G) (F · H₂)
(λ ζ₂ : invertible_2cell
          (essentially_surjective_is_eso_lift HG H₁ H₂
             α · G) H₂,
 (essentially_surjective_is_eso_lift_left HG H₁ H₂ α
  ▹ G) • α =
 rassociator F
   (essentially_surjective_is_eso_lift HG H₁ H₂ α) G
 • (F ◃ ζ₂))
  (essentially_surjective_is_eso_lift_right HG H₁ H₂ α)
 exact (essentially_surjective_is_eso_lift_eq HG H₁ H₂ α).
  Defined.

is_eso F

× fully_faithful_1cell m × invertible_2cell (f' · m) F

  (bicat_of_univ_cats,, has_pb_bicat_of_univ_cats)

  (bicat_of_univ_cats,, has_pb_bicat_of_univ_cats)
